    var lastUrl = window.location.href, initialHash;
    if (history.pushState) {
        window.onpopstate = function(e) {

            if (!e.state) {
                if (initialHash) {
                    //window.location.hash = 'test';
                    window.location.hash = initialHash.substring(1);
                }
                return
            }

                        if (document.location.href != lastUrl) {
                //alert(lastUrl + ' != ' + document.location.href);
                var newUrl = document.location.href;
                history.pushState({}, null, lastUrl);
                location.href = newUrl;
            }
                    }
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            var elementID;
            var zoneOnScreen = function(obj) {
                var rect = obj.getBoundingClientRect();
                var viewHeight = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight);
                return !(rect.bottom < 0 || rect.top - 500 - viewHeight >= 0);
            }
            
            var staticZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('staticbanner');
            if (staticZones) {
                for (var i = 0; i < staticZonesItems.length; i++) {
                    elementID = staticZonesItems[i].getAttribute('id');
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                        googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(
                            staticZones[elementID]['unit'],
                            elementID
                        ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                        googletag.display(elementID);
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();
                    });
                }
            }

            var lazyZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('lazybanner');
            if (lazyZonesItems.length > 0) {
                var lazyListener = function() {
                    for (var key in lazyZones) {
                        if (zoneOnScreen(document.getElementById(key))) {
                            // if banner from inside gallery, dont load it now
                            if (key != 'div-gpt-ad-1680693038182-0') {
                                googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                                    googletag.defineSlot(
                                        lazyZones[key]['unit'],
                                        lazyZones[key]['sizes'],
                                        key
                                    ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                                    googletag.display(key);
                                    if (true) { // false kad išjungti header biddingą
                                        let hb = !!googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(function(slot) {
                                            if(slot.getSlotElementId() === key){
                                                return !!stpd.vars.adUnitsRaw.filter(function (adunit) {
                                                    return adunit.path === slot.getAdUnitPath();
                                                }).length
                                            } else {return false;}
                                        }).length

                                        if (hb) {
                                            stpd.initializeAdUnit(key);
                                        } else {
                                            let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                            googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                        }
                                    } else {
                                        let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                        googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                    }
                                });
                                delete lazyZones[key];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };

                window.addEventListener('scroll', lazyListener);
                lazyListener();
            }
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var selectedOrderItem = document.getElementById('selectedOrderItem');
    selectedOrderItem.onclick = toggleOrderSelect;

    var elems = document.getElementsByClassName('result-item-v3');
    for(var i =0; i<elems.length; i++){
        elems[i].onclick = showLoadObject;
    }

    function showLoadObject(e){
        e = e || window.event;
        var btnCode;
        if ('object' === typeof e) {
            btnCode = e.button;
            switch (btnCode) {
                case 0:
                    var id = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    document.getElementById(id).style.display='block';
                    break;
            }
        }
    }

    function toggleOrderSelect(Event){
        Event.stopPropagation();
        Event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        selectedOrderItem.parentNode.className = 'search-select-order expanded-select hide';
    }

    function changeFrequency(value, id) {
        var children = document.getElementById('frequencySelect' + id).children;
        for (var i = 0; i< children.length; i++) {
            if (value == i) {
                children[i].classList.add('open');
            } else {
                children[i].classList.remove('open');
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('frequencyButton' + id).value = value;
    }

    let subscribeSearchTabs = document.querySelectorAll('.subscribe-search');
    for (let i = 0; i < subscribeSearchTabs.length; i++) {
        subscribeSearchTabs[i].addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            let element = this;
            promise.get('/ajax/checkUserLoggedIn/').then(function (error, data, xhr) {
                if (data == 1) {
                    location.href = element.getAttribute('data-url');
                } else {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: element.getAttribute('data-url')}).then(function (error, text, xhr) {
                        location.href = '/prisijungti/?subscribeSearch=1&return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1';
                    });
                }
            })
        })
    }

    var sorterEls = document.querySelectorAll(
        '.search-result-toolbar-v2__order__wrapper'
        + ', .search-result-toolbar-v3__order__wrapper'
        + ', .search-result-toolbar-v3__order__text'
        + ', .order-clickarea'
    )

    var mapClickEls = document.querySelectorAll('.map-clickarea');


    sorterEls.forEach(function(sorterEl) {
        sorterEl.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            Event.stopImmediatePropagation();
            var optionsList = document.querySelector('.search-select-order')
            if (optionsList.classList.contains('hide')) {
                optionsList.classList.remove('hide');
            } else {
                optionsList.classList.add('hide');
            }
        });
    })

    mapClickEls.forEach(function(mapClickEl) {
        mapClickEl.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            var mapLink = document.querySelector('.a-wrap-2 a').getAttribute('href')
            if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                ga('send', 'event', 'map-show', 'Click', 'from-list');gtag('event', 'map-show', {'event_category': 'from-list', 'event_action': 'Click'});
            }

            window.location.href = mapLink;
        });
    });

    var searchVersionEls = document.querySelectorAll('.toggle-search-version');
    searchVersionEls.forEach(function(searchVersionEl) {
        searchVersionEl.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            var searchVersionEl = e.currentTarget;
            var version = searchVersionEl.getAttribute('data-value');
            if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                var versionLabel = parseInt(version) === 2 ? 'small' : 'large';
                ga('send', 'event', 'search-version-switch-' + versionLabel, 'Click', 'from-list');gtag('event', 'search-version-switch-' + versionLabel, {'event_category': 'from-list', 'event_action': 'Click'});
            }
        });
    });

    function setVisited(elem) {
    }

    document.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
        toggleOrderSelect(Event);
    })

    var balloon = document.getElementById('countBalloon');
    var balloon2 = document.getElementById('countBalloon2');
    var saveAdvertButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.advert-controls-save-v2.action-button-js-hook');
    saveAdvertButtons.forEach(function(el) {
        el.addEventListener('click', saveAdvertAction)
    });

    function saveAdvertAction(event) {
        var saveAdvertButton = event.currentTarget;
        event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        if (event.preventDefault) {
            event.preventDefault();
        } else {
            event.returnValue = false;
        }

        var actionSave = true;
        var url = '/ajax/saveAdvert/';
        if (saveAdvertButton.classList.contains('remembered')) {
            actionSave = false;
            url = '/ajax/removeAdvert/';
        }

        var uniqueId = saveAdvertButton.getAttribute('data-id');
        promise.post(url, {uniqueId: uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
            if (error) {
                return;
            }

            if (!text) {
                return;
            }

            text=JSON.parse(text);
            if (text.error == 0) {
                if (actionSave) {
                    setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'saved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'saved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                } else {
                    setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'unsaved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'unsaved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                }

                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'balloon-count';
                    balloon.innerHTML = text.count;
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = '';
                    balloon2.innerHTML = '(' + text.count + ')';
                }

                var objRemembered = document.getElementById('objRemembered');
                if (objRemembered) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                var objRememberedDetails = document.getElementById('objRememberedDetails');
                if (objRememberedDetails) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                if (text && text.askAllowContact) {
                    location.href="/sutikimas-kontaktui-is-pardavejo/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=" + uniqueId;
                }
            } else if (text.toomuch == 1) {
                alert(text.msg);
                //saveAdvertButton.className = 'sticky-link';
            } else {
                if (text.register) {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: location.href + '&saveAdvert=' + uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
                        location.href = '/prisijungti/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=' + uniqueId + '&saveAdvert=2';
                    });
                }
                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'hide';
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = 'hide';
                }
            }
        });

        return false;
    }


    function setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.add('remembered');
    }

    function setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.remove('remembered');
    }

    function inIframe () {
        try {
            return window.self !== window.top;
        } catch (e) {
            return true;
        }
    }

    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            var elementID;
            var zoneOnScreen = function(obj) {
                var rect = obj.getBoundingClientRect();
                var viewHeight = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight);
                return !(rect.bottom < 0 || rect.top - 500 - viewHeight >= 0);
            }
            
            var staticZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('staticbanner');
            if (staticZones) {
                for (var i = 0; i < staticZonesItems.length; i++) {
                    elementID = staticZonesItems[i].getAttribute('id');
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                        googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(
                            staticZones[elementID]['unit'],
                            elementID
                        ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                        googletag.display(elementID);
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();
                    });
                }
            }

            var lazyZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('lazybanner');
            if (lazyZonesItems.length > 0) {
                var lazyListener = function() {
                    for (var key in lazyZones) {
                        if (zoneOnScreen(document.getElementById(key))) {
                            // if banner from inside gallery, dont load it now
                            if (key != 'div-gpt-ad-1680693038182-0') {
                                googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                                    googletag.defineSlot(
                                        lazyZones[key]['unit'],
                                        lazyZones[key]['sizes'],
                                        key
                                    ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                                    googletag.display(key);
                                    if (true) { // false kad išjungti header biddingą
                                        let hb = !!googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(function(slot) {
                                            if(slot.getSlotElementId() === key){
                                                return !!stpd.vars.adUnitsRaw.filter(function (adunit) {
                                                    return adunit.path === slot.getAdUnitPath();
                                                }).length
                                            } else {return false;}
                                        }).length

                                        if (hb) {
                                            stpd.initializeAdUnit(key);
                                        } else {
                                            let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                            googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                        }
                                    } else {
                                        let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                        googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                    }
                                });
                                delete lazyZones[key];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };

                window.addEventListener('scroll', lazyListener);
                lazyListener();
            }
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var selectedOrderItem = document.getElementById('selectedOrderItem');
    selectedOrderItem.onclick = toggleOrderSelect;

    var elems = document.getElementsByClassName('result-item-v3');
    for(var i =0; i<elems.length; i++){
        elems[i].onclick = showLoadObject;
    }

    function showLoadObject(e){
        e = e || window.event;
        var btnCode;
        if ('object' === typeof e) {
            btnCode = e.button;
            switch (btnCode) {
                case 0:
                    var id = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    document.getElementById(id).style.display='block';
                    break;
            }
        }
    }

    function toggleOrderSelect(Event){
        Event.stopPropagation();
        Event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        selectedOrderItem.parentNode.className = 'search-select-order expanded-select hide';
    }

    function changeFrequency(value, id) {
        var children = document.getElementById('frequencySelect' + id).children;
        for (var i = 0; i< children.length; i++) {
            if (value == i) {
                children[i].classList.add('open');
            } else {
                children[i].classList.remove('open');
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('frequencyButton' + id).value = value;
    }

    let subscribeSearchTabs = document.querySelectorAll('.subscribe-search');
    for (let i = 0; i < subscribeSearchTabs.length; i++) {
        subscribeSearchTabs[i].addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            let element = this;
            promise.get('/ajax/checkUserLoggedIn/').then(function (error, data, xhr) {
                if (data == 1) {
                    location.href = element.getAttribute('data-url');
                } else {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: element.getAttribute('data-url')}).then(function (error, text, xhr) {

                    });

            })
        })
    }

    var balloon = document.getElementById('countBalloon');
    var balloon2 = document.getElementById('countBalloon2');
    var saveAdvertButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.advert-controls-save-v2.action-button-js-hook');
    saveAdvertButtons.forEach(function(el) {
        el.addEventListener('click', saveAdvertAction)
    });

    function saveAdvertAction(event) {
        var saveAdvertButton = event.currentTarget;
        event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        if (event.preventDefault) {
            event.preventDefault();
        } else {
            event.returnValue = false;
        }

        var actionSave = true;
        var url = '/ajax/saveAdvert/';
        if (saveAdvertButton.classList.contains('remembered')) {
            actionSave = false;
            url = '/ajax/removeAdvert/';
        }

        var uniqueId = saveAdvertButton.getAttribute('data-id');
        promise.post(url, {uniqueId: uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
            if (error) {
                return;
            }

            if (!text) {
                return;
            }

            text=JSON.parse(text);
            if (text.error == 0) {
                if (actionSave) {
                    setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'saved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'saved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                } else {
                    setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'unsaved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'unsaved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                }

                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'balloon-count';
                    balloon.innerHTML = text.count;
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = '';
                    balloon2.innerHTML = '(' + text.count + ')';
                }

                var objRemembered = document.getElementById('objRemembered');
                if (objRemembered) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                var objRememberedDetails = document.getElementById('objRememberedDetails');
                if (objRememberedDetails) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                if (text && text.askAllowContact) {
                    location.href="/sutikimas-kontaktui-is-pardavejo/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=" + uniqueId;
                }
            } else if (text.toomuch == 1) {
                alert(text.msg);
                //saveAdvertButton.className = 'sticky-link';
            } else {
                if (text.register) {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: location.href + '&saveAdvert=' + uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
                        location.href = '/prisijungti/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=' + uniqueId + '&saveAdvert=2';
                    });
                }
                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'hide';
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = 'hide';
                }
            }
        });

        return false;
    }


    function setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.add('remembered');
    }

    function setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.remove('remembered');
    }

    function inIframe () {
        try {
            return window.self !== window.top;
        } catch (e) {
            return true;
        }
    }

    function onClickLuminor(e) {
        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
        if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
            ga('send', 'event', 'luminor_calc_21', 'Click', 'm-list_big_thumbs');gtag('event', 'luminor_calc_21', {'event_category': 'm-list_big_thumbs', 'event_action': 'Click'});
        }

        var uniqueId = e.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-uniqueId');
        window.location.href = '/luminor-skaiciuokle/?uniqueId=' + uniqueId + '&from=m-list_big_thumbs';
    }

    <script type="text/javascript">
        window.addEventListener('load', function() {
            var elementID;
            var zoneOnScreen = function(obj) {
                var rect = obj.getBoundingClientRect();
                var viewHeight = Math.max(document.documentElement.clientHeight, window.innerHeight);
                return !(rect.bottom < 0 || rect.top - 500 - viewHeight >= 0);
            }
            
            var staticZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('staticbanner');
            if (staticZones) {
                for (var i = 0; i < staticZonesItems.length; i++) {
                    elementID = staticZonesItems[i].getAttribute('id');
                    googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                        googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(
                            staticZones[elementID]['unit'],
                            elementID
                        ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                        googletag.display(elementID);
                        googletag.pubads().refresh();
                    });
                }
            }

            var lazyZonesItems = document.getElementsByClassName('lazybanner');
            if (lazyZonesItems.length > 0) {
                var lazyListener = function() {
                    for (var key in lazyZones) {
                        if (zoneOnScreen(document.getElementById(key))) {
                            // if banner from inside gallery, dont load it now
                            if (key != 'div-gpt-ad-1680693038182-0') {
                                googletag.cmd.push(function() {
                                    googletag.defineSlot(
                                        lazyZones[key]['unit'],
                                        lazyZones[key]['sizes'],
                                        key
                                    ).addService(googletag.pubads());
                                    googletag.display(key);
                                    if (true) { // false kad išjungti header biddingą
                                        let hb = !!googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(function(slot) {
                                            if(slot.getSlotElementId() === key){
                                                return !!stpd.vars.adUnitsRaw.filter(function (adunit) {
                                                    return adunit.path === slot.getAdUnitPath();
                                                }).length
                                            } else {return false;}
                                        }).length

                                        if (hb) {
                                            stpd.initializeAdUnit(key);
                                        } else {
                                            let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                            googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                        }
                                    } else {
                                        let slot = googletag.pubads().getSlots().filter(slot => slot.getSlotElementId() === key);
                                        googletag.pubads().refresh(slot);
                                    }
                                });
                                delete lazyZones[key];
                            }
                        }
                    }
                };

                window.addEventListener('scroll', lazyListener);
                lazyListener();
            }
        });
    </script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var selectedOrderItem = document.getElementById('selectedOrderItem');
    selectedOrderItem.onclick = toggleOrderSelect;

    var elems = document.getElementsByClassName('result-item-v3');
    for(var i =0; i<elems.length; i++){
        elems[i].onclick = showLoadObject;
    }

    function showLoadObject(e){
        e = e || window.event;
        var btnCode;
        if ('object' === typeof e) {
            btnCode = e.button;
            switch (btnCode) {
                case 0:
                    var id = this.getAttribute('data-id');
                    document.getElementById(id).style.display='block';
                    break;
            }
        }
    }

    function toggleOrderSelect(Event){
        Event.stopPropagation();
        Event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        selectedOrderItem.parentNode.className = 'search-select-order expanded-select hide';
    }

    function changeFrequency(value, id) {
        var children = document.getElementById('frequencySelect' + id).children;
        for (var i = 0; i< children.length; i++) {
            if (value == i) {
                children[i].classList.add('open');
            } else {
                children[i].classList.remove('open');
            }
        }

        document.getElementById('frequencyButton' + id).value = value;
    }

    let subscribeSearchTabs = document.querySelectorAll('.subscribe-search');
    for (let i = 0; i < subscribeSearchTabs.length; i++) {
        subscribeSearchTabs[i].addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            let element = this;
            promise.get('/ajax/checkUserLoggedIn/').then(function (error, data, xhr) {
                if (data == 1) {
                    location.href = element.getAttribute('data-url');
                } else {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: element.getAttribute('data-url')}).then(function (error, text, xhr) {
                        location.href = '/prisijungti/?subscribeSearch=1&return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1';
                    });
                }
            })
        })
    }

    var sorterEls = document.querySelectorAll(
        '.search-result-toolbar-v2__order__wrapper'
        + ', .search-result-toolbar-v3__order__wrapper'
        + ', .search-result-toolbar-v3__order__text'
        + ', .order-clickarea'
    )

    var mapClickEls = document.querySelectorAll('.map-clickarea');


    sorterEls.forEach(function(sorterEl) {
        sorterEl.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            Event.stopImmediatePropagation();
            var optionsList = document.querySelector('.search-select-order')
            if (optionsList.classList.contains('hide')) {
                optionsList.classList.remove('hide');
            } else {
                optionsList.classList.add('hide');
            }
        });
    })

    mapClickEls.forEach(function(mapClickEl) {
        mapClickEl.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
            var mapLink = document.querySelector('.a-wrap-2 a').getAttribute('href')
            if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                ga('send', 'event', 'map-show', 'Click', 'from-list');gtag('event', 'map-show', {'event_category': 'from-list', 'event_action': 'Click'});
            }

            window.location.href = mapLink;
        });
    });

    var searchVersionEls = document.querySelectorAll('.toggle-search-version');
    searchVersionEls.forEach(function(searchVersionEl) {
        searchVersionEl.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
            var searchVersionEl = e.currentTarget;
            var version = searchVersionEl.getAttribute('data-value');
            if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
                var versionLabel = parseInt(version) === 2 ? 'small' : 'large';
                ga('send', 'event', 'search-version-switch-' + versionLabel, 'Click', 'from-list');gtag('event', 'search-version-switch-' + versionLabel, {'event_category': 'from-list', 'event_action': 'Click'});
            }
        });
    });

    function setVisited(elem) {
    }

    document.addEventListener('click', function(Event) {
        toggleOrderSelect(Event);
    })

    var balloon = document.getElementById('countBalloon');
    var balloon2 = document.getElementById('countBalloon2');
    var saveAdvertButtons = document.querySelectorAll('.advert-controls-save-v2.action-button-js-hook');
    saveAdvertButtons.forEach(function(el) {
        el.addEventListener('click', saveAdvertAction)
    });

    function saveAdvertAction(event) {
        var saveAdvertButton = event.currentTarget;
        event.stopImmediatePropagation();
        if (event.preventDefault) {
            event.preventDefault();
        } else {
            event.returnValue = false;
        }

        var actionSave = true;
        var url = '/ajax/saveAdvert/';
        if (saveAdvertButton.classList.contains('remembered')) {
            actionSave = false;
            url = '/ajax/removeAdvert/';
        }

        var uniqueId = saveAdvertButton.getAttribute('data-id');
        promise.post(url, {uniqueId: uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
            if (error) {
                return;
            }

            if (!text) {
                return;
            }

            text=JSON.parse(text);
            if (text.error == 0) {
                if (actionSave) {
                    setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'saved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'saved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                } else {
                    setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton);
                    ga('send', 'event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', 'Click', 'unsaved');gtag('event', 'ar-mobile-search-remember-ad', {'event_category': 'unsaved', 'event_action': 'Click'});
                }

                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'balloon-count';
                    balloon.innerHTML = text.count;
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = '';
                    balloon2.innerHTML = '(' + text.count + ')';
                }

                var objRemembered = document.getElementById('objRemembered');
                if (objRemembered) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRemembered.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRemembered.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                var objRememberedDetails = document.getElementById('objRememberedDetails');
                if (objRememberedDetails) {
                    if (actionSave) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) + 1;
                    } else {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) - 1;
                    }

                    if (parseInt(objRememberedDetails.innerHTML) <= 0) {
                        objRememberedDetails.innerHTML = '0';
                    }
                }

                if (text && text.askAllowContact) {
                    location.href="/sutikimas-kontaktui-is-pardavejo/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=" + uniqueId;
                }
            } else if (text.toomuch == 1) {
                alert(text.msg);
                //saveAdvertButton.className = 'sticky-link';
            } else {
                if (text.register) {
                    promise.post('/ajax/setLastLocation/', {last_location: location.href + '&saveAdvert=' + uniqueId}).then(function(error, text, xhr) {
                        location.href = '/prisijungti/?return_url=%2Fbutai%2F%3Fobj%3D1&uniqueId=' + uniqueId + '&saveAdvert=2';
                    });
                }
                if (balloon) {
                    balloon.className = 'hide';
                }
                if (balloon2) {
                    balloon2.className = 'hide';
                }
            }
        });

        return false;
    }


    function setSavedOn(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.add('remembered');
    }

    function setSavedOff(saveAdvertButton) {
        saveAdvertButton.classList.remove('remembered');
    }

    function inIframe () {
        try {
            return window.self !== window.top;
        } catch (e) {
            return true;
        }
    }

    function onClickLuminor(e) {
        e.stopImmediatePropagation();
        if (typeof gtag === 'function') {
            ga('send', 'event', 'luminor_calc_21', 'Click', 'm-list_big_thumbs');gtag('event', 'luminor_calc_21', {'event_category': 'm-list_big_thumbs', 'event_action': 'Click'});
        }

        var uniqueId = e.currentTarget.getAttribute('data-uniqueId');
        window.location.href = '/luminor-skaiciuokle/?uniqueId=' + uniqueId + '&from=m-list_big_thumbs';
    }

    </script>
